     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h2 id="How_it_works" class="lb-none-v-margin lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> How it works</h2> 
       <div class="lb-txt-none lb-txt-lead lb-txt">
         IAM assists in creating roles and permissions 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>AWS IAM allows you to:</p> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a href="/iam/features/manage-users/">Manage IAM users&nbsp;</a>and <a href="/iam/features/managing-user-credentials/">their access</a> – You can create users in IAM, assign them individual security credentials (in other words, access keys, passwords, and <a href="/iam/features/mfa/">multi-factor authentication</a> devices), or request temporary security credentials to provide users access to AWS services and resources. You can manage permissions in order to control which operations a user can perform.</li> 
         <li><a href="/iam/features/manage-roles/">Manage IAM roles</a>&nbsp;and <a href="/iam/features/manage-permissions/">their permissions</a> – You can create roles in IAM and manage permissions to control which operations can be performed by the entity, or AWS service, that assumes the role. You can also define which entity is allowed to assume the role. In addition, you can use <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/console/iam/service-linked-role" target="_blank">service-linked roles</a> to delegate permissions to AWS services that create and manage AWS resources on your behalf.</li> 
         <li><a href="/identity/federation/">Manage federated users</a> and <a href="/iam/features/manage-permissions/">their permissions</a> – You can enable identity federation to allow existing identities (users, groups, and roles) in your enterprise to access the AWS Management Console, call AWS APIs, and access resources, without the need to create an IAM user for each identity. Use any identity management solution that supports <a href="/identity/saml/">SAML 2.0</a>, or use one of our federation samples (<a href="http://aws.amazon.com/code/4001165270590826" target="_blank">AWS Console SSO</a> or <a href="http://aws.amazon.com/code/1288653099190193" target="_blank">API federation</a>).</li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#fafafa;"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h2 id="Best_practices" class="lb-txt-bold lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Best practices</h2> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>AWS has a list of best practices to help IT professionals and developers manage access to AWS resources.<br /> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
         <div class="lb-border-horizontal lb-border-p lb-none-v-margin lb-tbl lb-tbl-header-centered" style="border-color:#F2F4F6;" data-is-sticky-header="false"> 
          <table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"> 
           <tbody> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-users/"><b>Users</b></a> – Create individual users.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-users/"><b>Groups</b></a> – Manage permissions with groups.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-permissions/"><b>Permissions</b></a> – Grant least privilege.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/cloudtrail/"><b>Auditing</b></a> – Turn on AWS CloudTrail.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/managing-user-credentials/"><b>Password</b></a> – Configure a strong password policy.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/mfa/"><b>MFA</b></a> – Enable MFA for privileged users.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-roles/"><b>Roles</b></a> – Use IAM roles for Amazon EC2 instances.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/identity/federation/"><b>Sharing</b></a> – Use IAM roles to share access.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSEC2/latest/UserGuide/iam-roles-for-amazon-ec2.html"><b>Rotate</b></a> – Rotate security credentials regularly.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="http://docs.aws.amazon.com/IAM/latest/UserGuide/PermissionsAndPolicies.html"><b>Conditions</b></a> – Restrict privileged access further with conditions.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-users/"><b>Root</b></a> – Reduce or remove use of root.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
           </tbody> 
          </table> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
         <div class="lb-video lb-video-p" data-lb-comp="video" data-placement="inPlace" data-youtube-id="YQsK4MtsELU" data-source="youtube" data-video-title="Become an IAM policy master in 60 minutes or less (55:35)">

  <div id="aws-page-content" class="lb-page-content lb-page-with-sticky-subnav" style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px;" data-page-alert-target="true"> 
   <main role="main"> 
    <div class="lb-bg-left-top-cover data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="margin-top:0px; background-image:url('//d1.awsstatic.com/rdsImages/ImgHead_RDS-Databases_Orange.5ddaa87c13ca6bfa79c4b14897188133e8acf4fe.jpg');" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="hero" data-da-so-version="1" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h1 id="Amazon_Relational_Database_Service_.28RDS.29" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-white lb-txt-44 lb-none-v-margin lb-h1-large lb-title" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px;"> Amazon Relational Database Service (RDS)</h1> 
       <div class="lb-none-pad lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
         <h3 id="Set_up.2C_operate.2C_and_scale_a_relational_database_in_the_cloud_with_just_a_few_clicks." class="lb-txt-light lb-txt-white lb-none-v-margin lb-h3 lb-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> Set up, operate, and scale a relational database in the cloud with just a few clicks.</h3> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-none-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
         <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_pdp_hero_cta" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
          <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-btn" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="cta1" data-da-so-version="1" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
           <a class="lb-btn-p-primary" href="https://console.aws.amazon.com/rds/home" role="button"> <span> Get started with Amazon RDS</span> </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_ribbon_below-hero" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
    </div> 
    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-small-v-margin lb-grid" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="intro" data-da-so-version="2text" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
       <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-small-align-left lb-mid-align-left lb-large-align-left lb-xlarge-align-left lb-txt-light lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt" style="color:#232f3e;"> 
        <p>Amazon Relational Database Service (Amazon RDS) makes it easy to set up, operate, and scale a relational database in the cloud. It provides cost-efficient and resizable capacity while automating time-consuming administration tasks such as hardware provisioning, database setup, patching and backups. It frees you to focus on your applications so you can give them the fast performance, high availability, security and compatibility they need.</p> 
        <p>Amazon RDS is available on several <a href="/rds/instance-types/">database instance types</a> - optimized for memory, performance or I/O - and provides you with six familiar database engines to choose from, including <a href="/rds/aurora/">Amazon Aurora</a>, <a href="/rds/postgresql/">PostgreSQL</a>, <a href="/rds/mysql/">MySQL</a>, <a href="/rds/mariadb/">MariaDB</a>, <a href="/rds/oracle/">Oracle&nbsp;Database</a>, and&nbsp;<a href="/rds/sqlserver/">SQL Server</a>. You can use the <a href="/dms/">AWS Database Migration Service</a> to easily migrate or replicate your existing databases to Amazon RDS.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
       <div class="lb-video lb-video-p" data-lb-comp="video" data-placement="inPlace" data-youtube-id="eMzCI7S1P9M" data-source="youtube" data-video-title="Understanding Amazon Relational Database Service (1:53)"> 
        <figure itemscope="true" itemtype="http://schema.org/VideoObject"> 
         <div class="video-js" poster="//d1.awsstatic.com/rdsImages/Understanding%20RDS.57625a0875163df908711a6eea4800f44b518df5.png"></div>

            Understanding Amazon Relational Database Service (1:53) 
          </div>

        </figure> 
       </div>

     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h1 id="Amazon_RDS_database_engines" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-28 lb-h1 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Amazon RDS database engines</h1>

        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-4"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/rds/sqlserver/"> <img alt="200x100_Microsoft-SQL-Server_Logo_v2" title="200x100_Microsoft-SQL-Server_Logo_v2" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/logos/rds/200x100_Microsoft-SQL-Server_Logo_v2.80f16c4207b8b79c1b13c8435868213a8b7131cc.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#f1f4f6;" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="benefits" data-da-so-version="4-3x3" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h1 id="Benefits" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-h1 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Benefits</h1> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Easy_to_administer" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Easy to administer</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Amazon RDS makes it easy to go from project conception to deployment. Use the <a href="https://console.aws.amazon.com/rds">Amazon RDS Management Console</a>, the <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/cli/latest/reference/rds/index.html">AWS RDS Command-Line Interface,</a> or simple <a href="http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonRDS/latest/APIReference/Welcome.html">API calls</a> to access the capabilities of a production-ready relational database in minutes. No need for infrastructure provisioning, and no need for installing and maintaining database software.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#administration">Learn more &raquo;</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Highly_scalable" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Highly scalable</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>You can <a href="/rds/details/#DB_Instance_Classes">scale your database's compute and storage resources</a> with only a few mouse clicks or an API call, often with no downtime. Many Amazon RDS engine types allow you to launch one or more <a href="/rds/features/#Scalability">Read Replicas</a> to offload read traffic from your primary database instance.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#scalability">Learn more &raquo;</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Available_and_durable" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Available and durable</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Amazon RDS runs on the same highly reliable infrastructure used by other Amazon Web Services. When you provision a <a href="/rds/details/multi-az/">Multi-AZ</a> DB Instance, Amazon RDS synchronously replicates the data to a standby instance in a different Availability Zone (AZ). Amazon RDS has many other features that enhance reliability for critical production databases, including automated backups, database snapshots, and automatic host replacement.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#ha">Learn more &raquo;</a><a href="/rds/details/multi-az/"></a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Fast" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Fast</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Amazon RDS supports the most demanding database applications. You can choose between two SSD-backed storage options: one optimized for high-performance OLTP applications, and the other for cost-effective general-purpose use. In addition, <a href="/rds/aurora/">Amazon Aurora</a> provides performance on par with commercial databases at 1/10th the cost.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#performance">Learn more &raquo;</a><br /> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Secure" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Secure</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Amazon RDS makes it easy to control network access to your database. Amazon RDS also lets you run your database instances in <a href="/vpc/">Amazon Virtual Private Cloud (Amazon VPC)</a>, which enables you to isolate your database instances and to connect to your existing IT infrastructure through an industry-standard encrypted IPsec VPN. Many Amazon RDS engine types offer encryption at rest and encryption in transit.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#security">Learn more &raquo;</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Inexpensive" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Inexpensive</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>You pay very low rates and only for the resources you actually consume. In addition, you benefit from the option of <a href="/rds/pricing/">On-Demand pricing</a> with no up-front or long-term commitments, or even lower hourly rates via our <a href="/rds/reserved-instances/">Reserved Instance pricing</a>.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#cost-effectiveness">Learn more &raquo;</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div id="mid_page"></div>

    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="use-cases" data-da-so-version="6-logos" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h2 id="Use_cases" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Use cases</h2> 
       <h3 id="Web_and_mobile_applications" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Web and mobile applications</h3> 
       <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>Web and mobile applications that are built to operate at very large scale need a database with high throughput, massive storage scalability, and high availability. Amazon RDS fulfills the needs of such highly demanding applications with room for future growth. Since Amazon RDS does not have any licensing constraints, it perfectly fits the variable usage pattern of these applications.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/solutions/case-studies/airbnb/"> <img alt="AirBnB logo pretzel-204x64" title="AirBnB logo pretzel-204x64" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/china/hp/change_size/AirBnB%20logo%20pretzel-204x64.1d56c32711170e167b2ae294f927bf83dd6c81f0.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <blockquote>
            Airbnb chose Amazon RDS because it simplifies much of the time-consuming administrative tasks typically associated with databases. Airbnb uses Multi-Availability Zone (Multi-AZ) deployment to further automate its database replication and augment data durability. Airbnb was able to complete its entire database migration to Amazon RDS with only 15 minutes of downtime. 
           <br /> 
          </blockquote> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <h3 id="Ecommerce_applications" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Ecommerce applications</h3> 
       <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>Amazon RDS offers small and large ecommerce businesses a flexible, secured, highly scalable, and low-cost database solution for online sales and retailing. Amazon RDS provides a managed database offering helping ecommerce companies meet PCI compliance and focus on building high quality customer experiences without worrying about managing the underlying database.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/solutions/case-studies/instacart/"> <img alt="Instacart" title="Instacart" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/product-marketing/AI/customers/Instacart.86952951559a736ac3e819e6a9616d69c1e7a0b7.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <blockquote>
            To avoid the complexities of building a new production database from scratch, Instacart turned to Amazon RDS for their new same-day grocery delivery service. The company can now add millions of new items to its database every month and its engineering team can focus on developing new features and improving the overall customer experience. 
           <br /> 
          </blockquote> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <h3 id="Mobile_and_online_games" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Mobile and online games</h3> 
       <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>Mobile and Online games need a database platform with high throughput and availability. Amazon RDS manages the database infrastructure so game developers don’t have to worry about provisioning, scaling, or monitoring database servers. Amazon RDS provides familiar database engines that can rapidly grow capacity to meet user demand.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/solutions/case-studies/bandai-namco-studios/"> <img alt="bandai" title="bandai" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/security-center/bandai.114b4caa516d1edbcc14f23a6e7fd75c067f7ec4.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <blockquote>
            Bandai Namco Studios uses Amazon RDS to provide better performance, lower costs, better security, and greater availability for their arcade, social and mobile games. Bandai Namco saw the benefit in terms of reductions in overhead, especially when it came to adding, modifying, and removing server resources. 
           <br /> 
          </blockquote> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

  <div id="aws-page-content" class="lb-page-content lb-page-with-sticky-subnav" style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px;" data-page-alert-target="true"> 
   <main role="main"> 
    <div class="lb-bg-left-top-cover data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="margin-top:0px; background-image:url('//d1.awsstatic.com/rdsImages/ImgHead_RDS-Databases_Orange.5ddaa87c13ca6bfa79c4b14897188133e8acf4fe.jpg');" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="hero" data-da-so-version="1" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h1 id="Amazon_Relational_Database_Service_.28RDS.29" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-white lb-txt-44 lb-none-v-margin lb-h1-large lb-title" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px;"> Amazon Relational Database Service (RDS)</h1> 
       <div class="lb-none-pad lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
         <h3 id="Set_up.2C_operate.2C_and_scale_a_relational_database_in_the_cloud_with_just_a_few_clicks." class="lb-txt-light lb-txt-white lb-none-v-margin lb-h3 lb-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> Set up, operate, and scale a relational database in the cloud with just a few clicks.</h3> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-none-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
         <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_pdp_hero_cta" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
          <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-btn" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="cta1" data-da-so-version="1" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
           <a class="lb-btn-p-primary" href="https://console.aws.amazon.com/rds/home" role="button"> <span> Get started with Amazon RDS</span> </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_ribbon_below-hero" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
    </div> 
    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-small-v-margin lb-grid" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="intro" data-da-so-version="2text" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
       <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-small-align-left lb-mid-align-left lb-large-align-left lb-xlarge-align-left lb-txt-light lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt" style="color:#232f3e;"> 
        <p>Amazon Relational Database Service (Amazon RDS) makes it easy to set up, operate, and scale a relational database in the cloud. It provides cost-efficient and resizable capacity while automating time-consuming administration tasks such as hardware provisioning, database setup, patching and backups. It frees you to focus on your applications so you can give them the fast performance, high availability, security and compatibility they need.</p> 
        <p>Amazon RDS is available on several <a href="/rds/instance-types/">database instance types</a> - optimized for memory, performance or I/O - and provides you with six familiar database engines to choose from, including <a href="/rds/aurora/">Amazon Aurora</a>, <a href="/rds/postgresql/">PostgreSQL</a>, <a href="/rds/mysql/">MySQL</a>, <a href="/rds/mariadb/">MariaDB</a>, <a href="/rds/oracle/">Oracle&nbsp;Database</a>, and&nbsp;<a href="/rds/sqlserver/">SQL Server</a>. You can use the <a href="/dms/">AWS Database Migration Service</a> to easily migrate or replicate your existing databases to Amazon RDS.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
       <div class="lb-video lb-video-p" data-lb-comp="video" data-placement="inPlace" data-youtube-id="eMzCI7S1P9M" data-source="youtube" data-video-title="Understanding Amazon Relational Database Service (1:53)"> 
        <figure itemscope="true" itemtype="http://schema.org/VideoObject"> 
         <div class="video-js" poster="//d1.awsstatic.com/rdsImages/Understanding%20RDS.57625a0875163df908711a6eea4800f44b518df5.png"></div> 
         <figcaption> 
          <div itemprop="name">
            Understanding Amazon Relational Database Service (1:53) 
          </div> 
         </figcaption> 
         <meta itemprop="embedUrl" content="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=eMzCI7S1P9M" /> 
        </figure> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-grid" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="special" data-da-so-version="3" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h1 id="Amazon_RDS_database_engines" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-28 lb-h1 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Amazon RDS database engines</h1> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-4"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/rds/aurora/"> <img alt="Aurora" title="Aurora" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/Products/product-name/product-icons/Aurora.a4e3560533c66b28b2ffdc350ccd9aaca2bf65c5.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-4"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/rds/postgresql/"> <img alt="200x100_PostgreSQL_Logo_v2" title="200x100_PostgreSQL_Logo_v2" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/logos/rds/200x100_PostgreSQL_Logo_v2.a18ae5300a6efebee36ecfcc1ab7e56d8b00bc07.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-4"> 
         <figure class="lb-img">

         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-4"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/rds/mariadb/"> <img alt="200x100_MariaDB_Logo_v2" title="200x100_MariaDB_Logo_v2" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/logos/rds/200x100_MariaDB_Logo_v2.f4a0fd7c0db2466f521b58f778fbfe05fe7a8da8.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-4"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/rds/oracle/"> <img alt="200x100_Oracle_Logo_v2" title="200x100_Oracle_Logo_v2" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/logos/rds/200x100_Oracle_Logo_v2.7d04f429e97ea6a194501e606c49842294f64e4e.png" /></a>

    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#f1f4f6;" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="benefits" data-da-so-version="4-3x3" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h1 id="Benefits" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-h1 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Benefits</h1> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Easy_to_administer" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Easy to administer</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Amazon RDS makes it easy to go from project conception to deployment. Use the <a href="https://console.aws.amazon.com/rds">Amazon RDS Management Console</a>, the <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/cli/latest/reference/rds/index.html">AWS RDS Command-Line Interface,</a> or simple <a href="http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonRDS/latest/APIReference/Welcome.html">API calls</a> to access the capabilities of a production-ready relational database in minutes. No need for infrastructure provisioning, and no need for installing and maintaining database software.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#administration">Learn more &raquo;</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Highly_scalable" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Highly scalable</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>You can <a href="/rds/details/#DB_Instance_Classes">scale your database's compute and storage resources</a> with only a few mouse clicks or an API call, often with no downtime. Many Amazon RDS engine types allow you to launch one or more <a href="/rds/features/#Scalability">Read Replicas</a> to offload read traffic from your primary database instance.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#scalability">Learn more &raquo;</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Available_and_durable" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Available and durable</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Amazon RDS runs on the same highly reliable infrastructure used by other Amazon Web Services. When you provision a <a href="/rds/details/multi-az/">Multi-AZ</a> DB Instance, Amazon RDS synchronously replicates the data to a standby instance in a different Availability Zone (AZ). Amazon RDS has many other features that enhance reliability for critical production databases, including automated backups, database snapshots, and automatic host replacement.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#ha">Learn more &raquo;</a><a href="/rds/details/multi-az/"></a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Fast" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Fast</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Amazon RDS supports the most demanding database applications. You can choose between two SSD-backed storage options: one optimized for high-performance OLTP applications, and the other for cost-effective general-purpose use. In addition, <a href="/rds/aurora/">Amazon Aurora</a> provides performance on par with commercial databases at 1/10th the cost.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#performance">Learn more &raquo;</a><br /> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Secure" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Secure</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Amazon RDS makes it easy to control network access to your database. Amazon RDS also lets you run your database instances in <a href="/vpc/">Amazon Virtual Private Cloud (Amazon VPC)</a>, which enables you to isolate your database instances and to connect to your existing IT infrastructure through an industry-standard encrypted IPsec VPN. Many Amazon RDS engine types offer encryption at rest and encryption in transit.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#security">Learn more &raquo;</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <h3 id="Inexpensive" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Inexpensive</h3> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>You pay very low rates and only for the resources you actually consume. In addition, you benefit from the option of <a href="/rds/pricing/">On-Demand pricing</a> with no up-front or long-term commitments, or even lower hourly rates via our <a href="/rds/reserved-instances/">Reserved Instance pricing</a>.</p> 
          <p><a href="/rds/details/#cost-effectiveness">Learn more &raquo;</a></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div>

    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="use-cases" data-da-so-version="6-logos" data-da-so-url="/rds"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h2 id="Use_cases" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Use cases</h2> 
       <h3 id="Web_and_mobile_applications" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Web and mobile applications</h3> 
       <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>Web and mobile applications that are built to operate at very large scale need a database with high throughput, massive storage scalability, and high availability. Amazon RDS fulfills the needs of such highly demanding applications with room for future growth. Since Amazon RDS does not have any licensing constraints, it perfectly fits the variable usage pattern of these applications.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/solutions/case-studies/airbnb/"> <img alt="AirBnB logo pretzel-204x64" title="AirBnB logo pretzel-204x64" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/china/hp/change_size/AirBnB%20logo%20pretzel-204x64.1d56c32711170e167b2ae294f927bf83dd6c81f0.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <blockquote>
            Airbnb chose Amazon RDS because it simplifies much of the time-consuming administrative tasks typically associated with databases. Airbnb uses Multi-Availability Zone (Multi-AZ) deployment to further automate its database replication and augment data durability. Airbnb was able to complete its entire database migration to Amazon RDS with only 15 minutes of downtime. 
           <br /> 
          </blockquote> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <h3 id="Ecommerce_applications" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Ecommerce applications</h3> 
       <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>Amazon RDS offers small and large ecommerce businesses a flexible, secured, highly scalable, and low-cost database solution for online sales and retailing. Amazon RDS provides a managed database offering helping ecommerce companies meet PCI compliance and focus on building high quality customer experiences without worrying about managing the underlying database.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/solutions/case-studies/instacart/"> <img alt="Instacart" title="Instacart" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/product-marketing/AI/customers/Instacart.86952951559a736ac3e819e6a9616d69c1e7a0b7.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <blockquote>
            To avoid the complexities of building a new production database from scratch, Instacart turned to Amazon RDS for their new same-day grocery delivery service. The company can now add millions of new items to its database every month and its engineering team can focus on developing new features and improving the overall customer experience. 
           <br /> 
          </blockquote> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <h3 id="Mobile_and_online_games" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Mobile and online games</h3> 
       <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>Mobile and Online games need a database platform with high throughput and availability. Amazon RDS manages the database infrastructure so game developers don’t have to worry about provisioning, scaling, or monitoring database servers. Amazon RDS provides familiar database engines that can rapidly grow capacity to meet user demand.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <a href="/solutions/case-studies/bandai-namco-studios/"> <img alt="bandai" title="bandai" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/security-center/bandai.114b4caa516d1edbcc14f23a6e7fd75c067f7ec4.png" /></a> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <blockquote>
            Bandai Namco Studios uses Amazon RDS to provide better performance, lower costs, better security, and greater availability for their arcade, social and mobile games. Bandai Namco saw the benefit in terms of reductions in overhead, especially when it came to adding, modifying, and removing server resources. 
           <br /> 
          </blockquote> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

    <div class="lb-bg-center-top-cover-no-repeat data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="margin-top:0px; background-image:url('//d1.awsstatic.com/redshift/ImgHead_Redshift.a907eba6129667b65e4b5459006f438ea7fc9922.jpg');" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="hero" data-da-so-version="1" data-da-so-url="/redshift"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <div class="lb-none-pad lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:30px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
         <h1 id="Amazon_Redshift" class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-txt-bold lb-txt-white lb-txt-44 lb-none-v-margin lb-h1-large lb-title" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> Amazon Redshift</h1> 
         <div class="lb-txt-normal lb-txt-none lb-txt-white lb-txt-lead lb-txt">
           The most popular and fastest cloud data warehouse 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-none-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
          <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
           <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_pdp_hero_cta" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
            <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-btn" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="button" data-da-so-version="1" data-da-so-url="/redshift"> 
             <a class="lb-btn-p-primary" href="https://console.aws.amazon.com/redshift/home" role="button"> <span> Get started with a free 2-month trial</span> </a> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
          <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
           <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-btn" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="button" data-da-so-version="2" data-da-so-url="/redshift">

    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-small-v-margin lb-grid" style="padding-bottom:0px; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="customers" data-da-so-version="2" data-da-so-url="/redshift"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
       <div class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-24 lb-txt" style="margin-top:20px;">
         More customers pick Amazon Redshift than any other cloud data warehouse 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-small-align-left lb-mid-align-left lb-large-align-left lb-xlarge-align-left lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt" style="color:#232f3e;"> 
        <p>Redshift powers analytical workloads for Fortune 500 companies, startups, and everything in between. Companies like Lyft have grown with Redshift from startups to multi-billion dollar enterprises.<br /> <a href="/redshift/customer-success/"><b>Learn more about Redshift customers&nbsp;&raquo;</b></a></p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-none-v-margin lb-rtxt" style="margin-top:30px;"> 
        <p><b>10's of thousands</b></p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-txt-20 lb-none-v-margin lb-rtxt" style="margin-top:0px;"> 
        <div>
          of customers use Amazon Redshift 
         <br /> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-tiny" style="margin-bottom:0px;">

        <a style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:25px;" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MS1zleTPmA0" target="_blank"> <img src="//d1.awsstatic.com/redshift/McDonalds.5bbad63d964babde1cfa488985548e48d9fd543c.svg" /> </a> 
       </figure> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-bg-center-bottom-contain-no-repeat data-attr-wrapper lb-grid" style="background-color:#f2f4f4; padding-top:30px; background-image:url('//d1.awsstatic.com/redshift/Layer_White_1440x75.16d0551b897491654e3d859b6839de8c7f363eaa.png'); margin-bottom:0px;" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="performance" data-da-so-version="4" data-da-so-url="/redshift"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
       <div class="lb-box"> 
        <h2 id="Deepest_integration_with_your_data_lake_and_AWS_services" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-24 lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Deepest integration with your data lake and AWS services</h2> 
        <div class="lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt"> 
         <p>No other data warehouse makes it as easy to gain new insights from all your data. With Redshift you can query petabytes of structured and semi-structured data across your data warehouse, operational database, and your data lake using standard SQL. Redshift lets you easily save the results of your queries back to your S3 data lake using open formats like Apache Parquet to further analyze from other analytics services like Amazon EMR, Amazon Athena, and Amazon SageMaker.<br /> </p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-border-p-feature lb-mid-pad lb-box" style="background-color:#FFFFFF; border-width:10px;"> 
        <figure class="lb-tiny-iblock lb-img"> 
         <div> 
          <img alt="Equinox" title="Equinox" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/redshift/Equinox_Logo.4fd45cf8e50968314e82d0da2cce5223cb9aac4c.png" /> 
         </div> 
        </figure> 
        <div class="lb-txt-20 lb-rtxt" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
         <p>&quot;By leveraging Redshift Spectrum's ability to query data directly into our Amazon S3 data lake, we have been able to easily integrate new data sources in hours, not days or weeks.&nbsp; This has not only reduced our time to insight, but helped us control our infrastructure costs.&quot;</p> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-txt-18 lb-rtxt" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
         <div> 
          <b>- Elliott Cordo</b> 
         </div> 
         <div> 
          <i>VP of Data Analytics, Equinox Fitness</i> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
       <figure class="lb-tiny-iblock lb-img"> 
        <div> 
         <img alt="Redshift Data Lake Integration" title="Redshift Data Lake Integration" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/re19/Redshift/Product-Page-Diagram_Redshift_Data-Lake-Integration@2x.b04dff434226a5b3e5e38159bbf610ee617a5655.png" /> 
        </div> 
       </figure> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div>

     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap">

          <b>FASTER&nbsp;</b>THAN OTHER CLOUD DATA WAREHOUSES 
         </div>

       </div>

      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
       <div class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-24 lb-txt" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;">
         Performance matters and Amazon Redshift is the fastest cloud data warehouse available 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-small-align-left lb-mid-align-left lb-large-align-left lb-xlarge-align-left lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt" style="color:#232f3e; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <p>Redshift is the world’s fastest cloud data warehouse and gets faster every year. For performance intensive workloads you can use the <a href="https://pages.awscloud.com/Redshift_RA3instances.html">new RA3 instances</a> to get up to 3x the performance of any cloud data warehouse.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-bg-center-top-contain-no-repeat data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#f2f4f4; padding-top:0px; background-image:url('//d1.awsstatic.com/redshift/Layer_White_1140x45.3ffd5ccf5100c106d41d514039d72d52da780015.png'); margin-bottom:0px;" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="datalake" data-da-so-version="6" data-da-so-url="/redshift"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
       <div class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-24 lb-txt" style="margin-top:90px;">
         Preview the next generation of Redshift with AQUA (Advanced Query Accelerator) 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-small-align-left lb-mid-align-left lb-large-align-left lb-xlarge-align-left lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt" style="color:#232f3e; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <p>AQUA is a new distributed and hardware accelerated cache that allows Redshift to run up to 10x faster than any other cloud data warehouse.<br /> <br /> Learn more about AQUA – Preview and <a href="https://pages.awscloud.com/AQUA_Preview.html" target="_blank">sign up today &raquo;</a><br /> </p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8">

    <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-grid" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="cost" data-da-so-version="5" data-da-so-url="/redshift"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
       <div class="lb-border-p lb-tiny-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-box" style="background-color:#FFFFFF; border-width:10px; border-color:#EAEDED; margin-top:60px;"> 
        <div class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-50 lb-none-v-margin lb-rtxt" style="color:#3B48CC;"> 
         <p><b>50%</b></p> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-txt-20 lb-none-v-margin lb-rtxt"> 
         <div> 
          <b>LESS EXPENSIVE&nbsp;</b>THAN ALL OTHER CLOUD DATA WAREHOUSES 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
       <div class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-24 lb-txt" style="margin-top:20px; margin-bottom:0px;">
         Amazon Redshift costs less to operate than any other cloud data warehouse 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-small-align-left lb-mid-align-left lb-large-align-left lb-xlarge-align-left lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt" style="color:#232f3e;"> 
        <p>Start small at $0.25 per hour and scale up to petabytes for under $1000 per terabyte per year. Pay only for what you use and know how much you'll spend with predictable monthly costs. Amazon Redshift is at least 50% less expensive than all other cloud data warehouses.</p> 
        <p>Scale and pay for storage and compute separately and get the optimal amount of storage and compute for diverse workloads. Choose the size of your Redshift cluster based on your performance requirements, and only pay for the storage that you use. The new managed storage automatically scales your data warehouse storage capacity without you having to add and pay for additional compute instances.<br /> </p> 
       </div> 
      </div>

       <h2 id="Use_cases" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Use cases</h2> 
       <div class="lb-none-v-margin lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="padding-top:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
         <h3 id="Business_intelligence" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Business intelligence</h3> 
         <div class="lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Redshift makes it simple and cost effective to run high performance queries on petabytes of structured data so that you can build powerful reports and dashboards using your existing business intelligence tools.</p> 
          <p>Learn how Intuit uses Redshift for business intelligence. <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=owJ-ipdTbko" target="_blank">Learn more &raquo;</a><br /> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
         <h3 id="Operational_analytics_on_business_events" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Operational analytics on business events</h3> 
         <div class="lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>Bring together structured data from your data warehouse and semi-structured data such as application logs from your S3 data lake to get real-time operational insights on your applications and systems.</p> 
          <p>Learn how Euclid uses Redshift for analytics.&nbsp; <a href="/solutions/case-studies/euclid/">Learn more &raquo;</a><br /> </p> 
         </div>

  <div id="aws-page-content" class="lb-page-content lb-page-with-sticky-subnav" style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px;" data-page-alert-target="true"> 
   <main role="main"> 
    <div class="lb-bg-left-top-cover data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#232f3e; background-image:url('//d1.awsstatic.com/product-marketing/S3/image-header_s3-2.6bf0d512939e43aba4fbd4185874e05ff0d236d2.png');" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="tile1" data-da-so-version="hero" data-da-so-url="/s3"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h1 id="Amazon_S3" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-white lb-none-v-margin lb-h1-large lb-title"> Amazon S3</h1> 
       <h3 id="Object_storage_built_to_store_and_retrieve_any_amount_of_data_from_anywhere" class="lb-txt-light lb-txt-white lb-small-v-margin lb-h3 lb-title" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:30px;"> Object storage built to store and retrieve any amount of data from anywhere</h3> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_pdp_hero_cta" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
          <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-tiny-iblock lb-small-show lb-btn" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="tile1" data-da-so-version="cta1" data-da-so-url="/s3"> 
           <a class="lb-btn-a-primary" href="https://s3.console.aws.amazon.com/s3/home" role="button"> <span> Get started with Amazon S3</span> </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-tiny-iblock lb-small-show lb-btn" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="tile1" data-da-so-version="cta2" data-da-so-url="/s3"> 
          <a class="lb-btn-a" href="https://pages.awscloud.com/ln_NAMER_AmazonS3-Contact-Us.html" role="button"> <span> Request more information</span> </a> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_ribbon_below-hero" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_s3_landing" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
     <div class="data-attr-wrapper lb-mid-pad lb-small-v-margin lb-grid" data-da-type="so" data-da-so-type="viewport" data-da-so-language="en" data-da-so-category="monitoring" data-da-so-name="tile2" data-da-so-version="intro" data-da-so-url="/s3"> 
      <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
       <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
        <div class="lb-tiny-align-left lb-small-align-left lb-mid-align-left lb-large-align-left lb-xlarge-align-left lb-txt-light lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt" style="color:#232f3e;"> 
         <p>Amazon Simple Storage Service (Amazon S3) is an object storage service that offers industry-leading scalability, data availability, security, and performance. This means customers of all sizes and industries can use it to store and protect any amount of data for a range of use cases, such as websites, mobile applications, backup and restore, archive, enterprise applications, IoT devices, and big data analytics. Amazon S3 provides easy-to-use management features so you can organize your data and configure finely-tuned access controls to meet your specific business, organizational, and compliance requirements. Amazon S3 is designed for 99.999999999% (11 9's) of durability, and stores data for millions of applications for companies all around the world.<br /> </p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
        <div class="lb-video lb-video-p" data-lb-comp="video" data-placement="inPlace" data-youtube-id="_I14_sXHO8U" data-source="youtube" data-video-title="Introduction to Amazon S3"> 
         <figure itemscope="true" itemtype="http://schema.org/VideoObject"> 
          <div class="video-js" poster="//d1.awsstatic.com/Data%20Lakes%20Storage%20Infrastructure/Data-Lake-Storage-Infrastructure_Video-Thumbnail_Amazon-S3.b3c1d2fe78a49278e4d012da0329b4ebe14dccb1.png"></div> 
          <figcaption> 
           <div itemprop="name">
             Introduction to Amazon S3 
           </div> 
          </figcaption> 
          <meta itemprop="embedUrl" content="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_I14_sXHO8U" /> 
         </figure> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#f1f4f6;"> 
      <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
       <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
        <h1 id="Benefits" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-h1 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Benefits</h1> 
        <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Industry-leading_performance.2C_scalability.2C_availability.2C_and_durability" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Industry-leading performance, scalability, availability, and durability</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Scale your storage resources up and down to meet fluctuating demands, without upfront investments or resource procurement cycles. Amazon S3 is designed for 99.999999999% (11 9’s) of data durability because it automatically creates and stores copies of all S3 objects across multiple systems. This means your data is available when needed and protected against failures, errors, and threats.</p> 
           <p><a href="/s3/faqs/#Durability_.26_Data_Protection" target="_blank">Learn about S3 data durability &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Wide_range_of_cost-effective_storage_classes" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Wide range of cost-effective storage classes</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Save costs without sacrificing performance by storing data across the <b>S3 Storage Classes</b>, which support different data access levels at corresponding rates. You can use <b>S3 Storage Class Analysis</b> to discover data that should move to a lower-cost storage class based on access patterns, and configure an <b>S3 Lifecycle</b> policy to execute the transfer. You can also store data with changing or unknown access patterns in <b>S3 Intelligent-Tiering</b>, which tiers objects based on changing access patterns and automatically delivers cost savings.</p> 
           <p><a href="/s3/cost-optimization/" target="_blank">Optimize costs using S3 &raquo;</a> and <a href="/s3/storage-classes/">learn more about the S3 Storage Classes &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Unmatched_security.2C_compliance.2C_and_audit_capabilities" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Unmatched security, compliance, and audit capabilities</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Store your data in Amazon S3 and secure it from unauthorized access with encryption features and access management tools. S3 is the only object storage service that allows you to block public access to all of your objects at the bucket or the account level with <b><a href="/s3/features/block-public-access/" target="_blank">S3 Block Public Access</a></b>. S3 maintains compliance programs, such as PCI-DSS, HIPAA/HITECH, FedRAMP, EU Data Protection Directive, and FISMA, to help you meet regulatory requirements. S3 integrates with <a href="/macie/" target="_blank">Amazon Macie</a> to discover and protect your sensitive data. AWS also supports numerous auditing capabilities to monitor access requests to your S3 resources.</p> 
           <p>Learn more about <a href="/s3/features/#Access_management_and_security">S3 security</a> and <a href="/compliance/">compliance &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Easily_manage_data_and_access_controls" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Easily manage data and access controls</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>S3 gives you robust capabilities to manage access, cost, replication, and data protection. S3 Access Points make it easy to manage data access with specific permissions for your applications using a shared data set. S3 Replication features manage data replication within the region or to other regions. S3 Batch Operations helps manage large scale changes across billions of objects. S3 integration with Amazon Macie automatically provides an inventory of buckets and continually evaluates your S3 buckets to alert you to any unencrypted buckets, publicly accessible buckets, or buckets shared with AWS accounts. Since S3 works with AWS Lambda, you can log activities, define alerts, and automate workflows without managing additional infrastructure.</p> 
           <p><a href="/s3/features/#Storage_management_and_monitoring">Learn more about S3 storage management features &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Query-in-place_services_for_analytics_" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Query-in-place services for analytics </h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Run big data analytics across your S3 objects (and other data sets in AWS) with our query-in-place services. Use <b>Amazon Athena</b> to query S3 data with standard SQL expressions and <b>Amazon Redshift Spectrum</b> to analyze data that is stored across your AWS data warehouses and S3 resources. You can also use <b>S3 Select </b>to retrieve subsets of object data, instead of the entire object, and improve query performance by up to 400%.</p> 
           <p><a href="/s3/features/#Query_in_place">Learn more about query in place &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Most_supported_cloud_storage_service" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Most supported cloud storage service</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Store and protect your data in Amazon S3 by working with a partner from the <b>AWS Partner Network (APN)</b> — the largest community of technology and consulting cloud services providers. The APN recognizes migration partners that transfer data to Amazon S3 and storage partners that offer S3-integrated solutions for primary storage, backup and restore, archive, and disaster recovery. You can also purchase an AWS-integrated solution directly from the <b>AWS Marketplace</b>, which lists over 250 storage-specific offerings.</p> 
           <p><a href="/backup-recovery/partner-solutions/">Learn about the APN</a> and<a href="https://aws.amazon.com/marketplace"> AWS Marketplace &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div id="mid_page"></div> 
     <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_banner_product-mid_page" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
     </div> 
     <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-small-v-margin lb-grid"> 
      <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
       <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
        <h2 id="How_it_works_.E2.80.94_S3_Access_Points" class="lb-txt-28 lb-none-v-margin lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> How it works — S3 Access Points</h2> 
        <figure class="lb-img"> 
         <div> 
          <img alt="Diagram_S3_Access_Points" title="Diagram_S3_Access_Points" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/re19/Westeros/Diagram_S3_Access_Points.fa88c474dc1073aede962aaf3a6af2d6b02be933.png" /> 
         </div> 
        </figure> 
        <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p><b><a name="preview"></a>&nbsp;</b>Amazon S3 Access Points simplifies managing data access at scale for applications using shared data sets on S3. With S3 Access Points, you can now easily create hundreds of access points per bucket, representing a new way of provisioning access to shared data sets. Access Points provide a customized path into a bucket, with a unique hostname and access policy that enforces the specific permissions and network controls for any request made through the access point.</p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#f1f4f6;"> 
      <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
       <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
        <h2 id="Use_cases" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Use cases</h2> 
        <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Backup_and_restore" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Backup and restore</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Build scalable, durable, and secure backup and restore solutions with Amazon S3 and other AWS services, such as <b>S3 Glacier</b>, <b>Amazon EFS</b>, and <b>Amazon EBS</b>, to augment or replace existing on-premises capabilities. AWS and APN partners can help you meet Recovery Time Objectives (RTO), Recovery Point Objectives (RPO), and compliance requirements. With AWS, you can back up data already in the AWS Cloud or use<b> AWS Storage Gateway</b>, a hybrid storage service, to send backups of on-premises data to AWS.</p> 
           <p><a href="/backup-restore/">Learn more about backup and restore &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Disaster_recovery_.28DR.29" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Disaster recovery (DR)</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Protect critical data, applications, and IT systems that are running in the AWS Cloud or in your on-premises environment without incurring the expense of a second physical site. With Amazon S3 storage, <b>S3 Cross-Region Replication</b>, and other AWS compute, networking, and database services, you can create DR architectures in order to quickly and easily recover from outages caused by natural disasters, system failures, and human errors.</p> 
           <p><a href="/disaster-recovery/"> Learn more about DR &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Archive" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Archive</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Retire physical infrastructure, and archive data with <b>S3 Glacier</b> and <b>S3 Glacier Deep Archive</b>. These S3 Storage Classes retain objects long-term at the lowest rates. Simply create an S3 Lifecycle policy to archive objects throughout their lifecycles, or upload objects directly to the archival storage classes. With <b>S3 Object Lock</b>, you can apply retention dates to objects to protect them from deletions, and meet compliance requirements. Unlike tape libraries, S3 Glacier lets you restore archived objects in as little as one minute for expedited retrievals and 3-5 hours for standard retrievals. Bulk data restores from S3 Glacier and all restores from S3 Glacier Deep Archive are completed within 12 hours.</p> 
           <p><a href="/glacier/">Learn more about archiving &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Data_lakes_and_big_data_analytics" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Data lakes and big data analytics</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Accelerate innovation by building a <a href="/products/storage/data-lake-storage/" target="_blank">data lake on Amazon S3</a>, and extract valuable insights using query-in-place, analytics, and machine learning tools. As your data lake grows, use S3 Access Points to easily configure access to your data, with specific permissions for each application or sets of applications. You can also use <b>AWS Lake Formation </b>to quickly create a data lake, and centrally define and enforce security, governance, and auditing policies. The service collects data across your databases and S3 resources, moves it into a new data lake in Amazon S3, and cleans and classifies it using machine learning algorithms. All AWS resources can be scaled up to accommodate your expanding data stores&nbsp;— without upfront investments.</p> 
           <p>Learn more about building a <a href="/products/storage/data-lake-storage/" target="_blank">data lake on Amazon S3</a>&nbsp;and <a href="/lake-formation/">AWS Lake Formation &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Hybrid_cloud_storage" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Hybrid cloud storage</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p><b>AWS Storage Gateway</b>&nbsp;lets you seamlessly connect and extend your on-premises applications to AWS Storage all while caching data locally for low-latency access. You can also automate data transfers between on-premises storage and Amazon S3 by using <b>AWS DataSync</b>, which can transfer data at speeds up to 10 times faster than open-source tools. You can also transfer files directly into and out of Amazon S3 with<b>&nbsp;</b>the<b> AWS Transfer Family&nbsp;</b>— a fully managed, simple, and seamless service that enables secure file exchanges with third parties using SFTP, FTPS, and FTP.&nbsp;Another way to enable a hybrid cloud storage environment is to work with a gateway provider from the APN.</p> 
           <p>Learn more about <a href="/storagegateway/" target="_blank">AWS Storage Gateway &raquo;</a> , <a href="/datasync/" target="_blank">AWS DataSync</a>&nbsp;&raquo; ,&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="/aws-transfer-family/" target="_blank">AWS Transfer Family &raquo;</a>&nbsp;<br /> </p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
          <h3 id="Cloud-native_applications" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Cloud-native applications</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Build fast, cost-effective mobile and internet-based applications by using AWS services and Amazon S3 to store development and production data shared by the microservices that make up cloud-native applications. With Amazon S3, you can upload any amount of data and access it anywhere in order to deploy applications faster and reach more end users. Storing data in Amazon S3 means you have access to the latest AWS developer tools, S3 API, and services for machine learning and analytics to innovate and optimize your cloud-native applications.</p> 
           <p><a href="/products/storage/object-storage-for-cloud-native-applications/" target="_blank">Learn more about cloud-native applications &raquo;</a></p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_tiles_full_page" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
     </div> 
     <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-small-v-margin lb-grid"> 
      <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
       <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
        <h2 id="Case_studies" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-28 lb-none-v-margin lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Case studies</h2> 
        <div class="lb-xb-grid-wrap" style="margin-top:1px;"> 
         <div class="lb-xb-grid lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-tiny-xb-1 lb-small-xb-2 lb-large-xb-4"> 
          <div class="lb-xbcol"> 
           <figure class="lb-img"> 
            <a href="/solutions/case-studies/georgia-pacific/" target="_blank"> </a> 
            <a href="/solutions/case-studies/georgia-pacific/"><img alt="Georgia-Pacific" title="Georgia-Pacific" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/case-studies/US/GP%20resize.eb8f2c55583fec8604358d96927dd5d630b5cb4e.jpg" /></a> 
           </figure> 
           <div class="lb-txt-light lb-txt-none lb-txt-16 lb-txt" style="color:#232f3e;">
             Georgia-Pacific builds a central data lake based on Amazon S3, allowing it to efficiently ingest and analyze structured and unstructured data at scale. 
           </div> 
          </div> 
          <div class="lb-xbcol"> 
           <figure class="lb-img"> 
            <a href="/solutions/case-studies/nasdaq-case-study/" target="_blank"> </a> 
            <a href="/solutions/case-studies/nasdaq-case-study/"><img alt="Nasdaq" title="Nasdaq" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/logos/600x400_logos/600x400_Nasdaq_Logo.8c68fa0643aef73eba95543fff39f1da560986f7.png" /></a> 
           </figure> 
           <div class="lb-txt-light lb-txt-none lb-txt-16 lb-txt" style="color:#232f3e;">
             Nasdaq stores up to seven years of data in Amazon S3 Glacier to meet industry regulation and compliance requirements. With AWS, the company is enabled to restore data while optimizing its long-term storage costs. 
           </div> 
          </div> 
          <div class="lb-xbcol"> 
           <figure class="lb-img"> 
            <a href="/solutions/case-studies/sysco/" target="_blank"> </a>

           </figure> 
           <div class="lb-txt-light lb-txt-none lb-txt-16 lb-txt" style="color:#232f3e;">
             Sysco consolidates its data into a single data lake built on Amazon S3 and Amazon S3 Glacier to run analytics on its data and gain business insights. 
           </div> 
          </div> 
          <div class="lb-xbcol"> 
           <figure class="lb-img"> 
            <a href="/solutions/case-studies/nielsen-case-study/" target="_blank"> </a> 
            <a href="/solutions/case-studies/nielsen-case-study/"><img alt="Nielsen" title="Nielsen" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/logos/600x400_Nielsen_Logo.1f74e606e15429c533b09026514881a8a94d0e8d.png" /></a> 
           </figure> 
           <div class="lb-txt-light lb-txt-none lb-txt-16 lb-txt" style="color:#232f3e;">
             Nielsen built a new, cloud-native local television rating platform capable of storing 30 petabytes of data in Amazon S3 and leveraging Amazon Redshift, AWS Lambda, and Amazon EMR. 
           </div>

       <h2 id="Ready_to_get_started.3F" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-28 lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Ready to get started?</h2> 
       <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <div> 
           <img alt="Product-Page_Standard-Icons_01_Product-Features_SqInk" title="Product-Page_Standard-Icons_01_Product-Features_SqInk" src="//d1.awsstatic.com/webteam/product-pages/Product-Page_Standard-Icons_01_Product-Features_SqInk.a8d5666758afc5121b4eb818ae18126031c4b61e.png" /> 
          </div> 
         </figure> 
         <div class="lb-tiny-align-center lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-txt">
           Check out S3 features 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-tiny-align-center lb-none-v-margin lb-rtxt"> 
          <p style="text-align: center;">Learn more about features for data management, security, access management, analytics, and more.<br /> </p> 
         </div> 
         <a class="lb-tiny-align-center lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-blue-link lb-txt" href="/s3/features/"> Learn more&nbsp;<i class="icon-angle-double-right"></i></a> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
         <figure class="lb-img"> 
          <div>

          </div>

           Sign up for a free account

          <p style="text-align: center;">Instantly get access to the AWS Free Tier and start experimenting with Amazon S3.&nbsp;</p>
