  <div id="aws-page-content" class="lb-page-content lb-page-with-sticky-subnav" style="padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px;" data-page-alert-target="true"> 
   <main role="main"> 
    <div class="lb-bg-left-top-cover lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="margin-top:0px; background-image:url('//d1.awsstatic.com/Products/product-name/Images/ImgHead_Generic_B2.643d561e48f5121a6320802cb5607c959adb8a4d.jpg');"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h1 id="AWS_Identity_and_Access_Management_.28IAM.29" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-white lb-none-v-margin lb-h1 lb-title" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px;"> AWS Identity and Access Management (IAM)</h1> 
       <div class="lb-txt-light lb-txt-none lb-txt-white lb-txt-20 lb-txt">
         Securely manage access to AWS services and resources 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-none-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap" style="margin-top:10px; margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
         <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_pdp_hero_cta" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
          <div class="lb-btn"> 
           <a class="lb-btn-a-primary" href="https://console.aws.amazon.com/iam/home" role="button"> <span> Get started with AWS IAM</span> </a> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-6"> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_ribbon_below-hero" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-16"> 
       <div class="lb-txt-16 lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>AWS Identity and Access Management (IAM) enables you to manage access to AWS services and resources securely. Using IAM, you can create and manage AWS users and groups, and use permissions to allow and deny their access to AWS resources.</p> 
        <p>IAM is a feature of your AWS account offered at no additional charge. You will be charged only for use of other AWS services by your users.</p> 
        <p>To get started using IAM, or if you have already registered with AWS, go to the <a href="https://console.aws.amazon.com/iam/home">AWS Management Console</a> and get started with these <a href="http://docs.aws.amazon.com/IAM/latest/UserGuide/IAMBestPractices.html">IAM Best Practices</a>.&nbsp;</p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-8"> 
       <div class="lb-video lb-video-p" data-lb-comp="video" data-placement="inPlace" data-youtube-id="Ul6FW4UANGc" data-source="youtube" data-video-title="AWS IAM Overview (2:15)"> 
        <figure itemscope="true" itemtype="http://schema.org/VideoObject"> 
         <div class="video-js"></div> 
         <figcaption> 
          <div itemprop="name">
            AWS IAM Overview (2:15) 
          </div> 
         </figcaption> 
         <meta itemprop="embedUrl" content="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Ul6FW4UANGc" /> 
        </figure> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#fafafa;"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h2 id="Use_cases" class="lb-txt-bold lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Use cases</h2> 
       <div class="lb-xb-grid-wrap" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-xb-grid lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-tiny-xb-1 lb-mid-xb-2"> 
         <div class="lb-xbcol"> 
          <h3 id="Fine-grained_access_control_to_AWS_resources" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Fine-grained access control to AWS resources</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>IAM enables <a href="/iam/features/manage-users/">your users</a> to <a href="/iam/features/manage-permissions/">control access</a> to AWS service APIs and to specific resources. IAM also enables you to add <a href="/iam/features/manage-permissions/">specific conditions</a> such as time of day to control how a user can use AWS, their originating IP address, whether they are using SSL, or whether they have authenticated with a <a href="/iam/features/mfa/">multi-factor authentication device</a>.<br /> </p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-xbcol"> 
          <h3 id="Multi-factor_authentication_for_highly_privileged_users" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Multi-factor authentication for highly privileged users</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>Protect your AWS environment by using <a href="/iam/features/mfa/">AWS MFA</a>, a security feature available at no extra cost that augments user name and password credentials. MFA requires users to prove physical possession of a hardware MFA token or MFA-enabled mobile device by providing a valid MFA code.<br /> </p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-xb-grid-wrap"> 
        <div class="lb-xb-grid lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-tiny-xb-1 lb-mid-xb-2"> 
         <div class="lb-xbcol"> 
          <h3 id="Analyze_access" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Analyze access</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>IAM helps you <a href="/iam/features/analyze-access/">analyze access</a> across your AWS environment. Your security teams and administrators can quickly validate that your policies only provide the intended public and cross-account access to your resources. You can also easily identify and refine your policies to allow access to only the services being used. This helps you to better adhere to the principle of least privilege.</p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <div class="lb-xbcol"> 
          <h3 id="Integrate_with_your_corporate_directory" class="lb-txt-bold lb-txt-none lb-txt-18 lb-h3 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Integrate with your corporate directory</h3> 
          <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
           <p>IAM can be used to grant your employees and applications <a href="/identity/federation/">federated access</a> to the AWS Management Console and AWS service APIs, using your existing identity systems&nbsp;such as Microsoft Active Directory. You can use any <a href="http://docs.aws.amazon.com/IAM/latest/UserGuide/IdP-solution-providers.html" target="_blank">identity management</a> solution that supports <a href="/identity/saml/">SAML 2.0</a>, or feel free to use one of our federation samples (<a href="http://aws.amazon.com/code/4001165270590826" target="_blank">AWS Console SSO</a> or <a href="http://aws.amazon.com/code/1288653099190193" target="_blank">API federation</a>).<br /> </p> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div id="mid_page"></div> 
    <div class="lb-mbox js-mbox" data-lb-comp="mbox" data-mbox="en_banner_product-mid_page" data-lb-comp-ignore="true"> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h2 id="How_it_works" class="lb-none-v-margin lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> How it works</h2> 
       <div class="lb-txt-none lb-txt-lead lb-txt">
         IAM assists in creating roles and permissions 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
        <p>AWS IAM allows you to:</p> 
        <ul> 
         <li><a href="/iam/features/manage-users/">Manage IAM users&nbsp;</a>and <a href="/iam/features/managing-user-credentials/">their access</a> – You can create users in IAM, assign them individual security credentials (in other words, access keys, passwords, and <a href="/iam/features/mfa/">multi-factor authentication</a> devices), or request temporary security credentials to provide users access to AWS services and resources. You can manage permissions in order to control which operations a user can perform.</li> 
         <li><a href="/iam/features/manage-roles/">Manage IAM roles</a>&nbsp;and <a href="/iam/features/manage-permissions/">their permissions</a> – You can create roles in IAM and manage permissions to control which operations can be performed by the entity, or AWS service, that assumes the role. You can also define which entity is allowed to assume the role. In addition, you can use <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/console/iam/service-linked-role" target="_blank">service-linked roles</a> to delegate permissions to AWS services that create and manage AWS resources on your behalf.</li> 
         <li><a href="/identity/federation/">Manage federated users</a> and <a href="/iam/features/manage-permissions/">their permissions</a> – You can enable identity federation to allow existing identities (users, groups, and roles) in your enterprise to access the AWS Management Console, call AWS APIs, and access resources, without the need to create an IAM user for each identity. Use any identity management solution that supports <a href="/identity/saml/">SAML 2.0</a>, or use one of our federation samples (<a href="http://aws.amazon.com/code/4001165270590826" target="_blank">AWS Console SSO</a> or <a href="http://aws.amazon.com/code/1288653099190193" target="_blank">API federation</a>).</li> 
        </ul> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="lb-mid-pad lb-none-v-margin lb-grid" style="background-color:#fafafa;"> 
     <div class="lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
      <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
       <h2 id="Best_practices" class="lb-txt-bold lb-h2 lb-title" style="color:#232f3e;"> Best practices</h2> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-24"> 
         <div class="lb-rtxt"> 
          <p>AWS has a list of best practices to help IT professionals and developers manage access to AWS resources.<br /> </p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="lb-grid lb-row lb-row-max-large lb-snap lb-gutter-mid" style="margin-bottom:0px;"> 
        <div class="lb-col lb-tiny-24 lb-mid-12"> 
         <div class="lb-border-horizontal lb-border-p lb-none-v-margin lb-tbl lb-tbl-header-centered" style="border-color:#F2F4F6;" data-is-sticky-header="false"> 
          <table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"> 
           <tbody> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-users/"><b>Users</b></a> – Create individual users.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-users/"><b>Groups</b></a> – Manage permissions with groups.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-permissions/"><b>Permissions</b></a> – Grant least privilege.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/cloudtrail/"><b>Auditing</b></a> – Turn on AWS CloudTrail.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/managing-user-credentials/"><b>Password</b></a> – Configure a strong password policy.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/mfa/"><b>MFA</b></a> – Enable MFA for privileged users.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-roles/"><b>Roles</b></a> – Use IAM roles for Amazon EC2 instances.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/identity/federation/"><b>Sharing</b></a> – Use IAM roles to share access.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AWSEC2/latest/UserGuide/iam-roles-for-amazon-ec2.html"><b>Rotate</b></a> – Rotate security credentials regularly.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="http://docs.aws.amazon.com/IAM/latest/UserGuide/PermissionsAndPolicies.html"><b>Conditions</b></a> – Restrict privileged access further with conditions.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
            <tr> 
             <td width="623" valign="middle" style="text-align: left;" height="14"><p><a href="/iam/features/manage-users/"><b>Root</b></a> – Reduce or remove use of root.</p> </td> 
            </tr> 
           </tbody> 
          </table> 
         </div> 
        </div>
